lt_lt_cv_sys_global_symbol_to_c_name_address='"sed -n -e '\''s/^: \\([^ ]*\\) \$/  {\\\"\\1\\\", (lt_ptr) 0},/p'\'' -e '\''s/^[BCDEGRST] \\([^ ]*\\) \\([^ ]*\\)\$/  {\"\\2\", (lt_ptr) \\&\\2},/p'\''"'
lt_lt_cv_sys_global_symbol_to_cdecl='"sed -n -e '\''s/^. .* \\(.*\\)\$/extern int \\1;/p'\''"'
